I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] S3 Content-Encoding header not persisted on objects
## Service

S3

## API Action / Feature

PutObject, GetObject, HeadObject — `Content-Encoding` header handling

## AWS Documentation

- https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/API_PutObject.html (`Content-Encoding` request header)
- https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/API_HeadObject.html (`Content-Encoding` response header)
- https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/API_GetObject.html (`Content-Encoding` response header)

## Why is this needed?

When an S3 object is uploaded with a `Content-Encoding` header (e.g., `gzip`, `application/zstd+multipart`), AWS S3 stores this metadata and returns it in subsequent `HeadObject` and `GetObject` responses. Applications use `Content-Encoding` to determine how to decode the object body.

Currently, floci receives the `Content-Encoding` header in `S3Controller.putObject()` (line 286) but only uses it for `decodeAwsChunked()` — it is **never stored** on the `S3Object` model. As a result, `HeadObject` and `GetObject` responses return `null` for `Content-Encoding`, causing `NullPointerException` in applications that expect it to be present.


## Expected behavior

```bash
# Upload object with Content-Encoding
aws s3api put-object \
  --bucket my-bucket \
  --key test.bin \
  --body test.bin \
  --content-encoding "application/zstd+multipart" \
  --content-type "application/java-aot" \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566

# HeadObject should return Content-Encoding
aws s3api head-object \
  --bucket my-bucket \
  --key test.bin \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566
# Expected: ContentEncoding: "application/zstd+multipart"

# GetObject should also return Content-Encoding
aws s3api get-object \
  --bucket my-bucket \
  --key test.bin \
  output.bin \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566
# Expected: ContentEncoding: "application/zstd+multipart" in response
```

## Actual behavior

`HeadObject` and `GetObject` responses do not include `Content-Encoding`, even when it was set during `PutObject`. The AWS SDK returns `null` for `contentEncoding()`, causing:

```
java.lang.NullPointerException: Cannot invoke "String.equals(Object)" because the return value of
"software.amazon.awssdk.services.s3.model.HeadObjectResponse.contentEncoding()" is null
```

## Root cause

In `S3Controller.java`, the `putObject` method receives `@HeaderParam("Content-Encoding") String contentEncoding` (line 286), but `s3Service.putObject()` does not accept or store it. The `S3Object` model class has no `contentEncoding` field.

## Are you willing to contribute a PR?

Yes

</pr_description>

   122	    private static String computeETag(byte[] data) {
   123	        try {
   124	            var md = java.security.MessageDigest.getInstance("MD5");
   125	            byte[] digest = md.digest(data);
   126	            var sb = new StringBuilder("\"");
   127	            for (byte b : digest) {
   128	                sb.append(String.format("%02x", b));
   129	            }
   130	            sb.append("\"");
   131	            return sb.toString();
   132	        } catch (java.security.NoSuchAlgorithmException e) {
   133	            return "\"\"";
   134	        }
   135	    }

    42	/**
    43	 * S3 controller handling REST-style S3 API requests.
    44	 * Routes: /{bucket} for bucket ops, /{bucket}/{key+} for object ops.
    45	 */
    46	@Path("/")
    47	public class S3Controller {
    48	
    49	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(S3Controller.class);
    50	    private static final DateTimeFormatter ISO_FORMAT = DateTimeFormatter.ISO_INSTANT;
    51	    private static final DateTimeFormatter RFC_822 = DateTimeFormatter
    52	            .ofPattern("EEE, dd MMM yyyy HH:mm:ss z", Locale.US)
    53	            .withZone(ZoneId.of("GMT"));
    54	
    55	    private final S3Service s3Service;
    56	    private final S3SelectService s3SelectService;
    57	    private final RegionResolver regionResolver;
    58	
    59	    @Inject
    60	    public S3Controller(S3Service s3Service, S3SelectService s3SelectService,
    61	                        RegionResolver regionResolver) {
    62	        this.s3Service = s3Service;
    63	        this.s3SelectService = s3SelectService;
    64	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    // --- Bucket operations ---
    68	
    69	    @GET
    70	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
    71	    public Response listBuckets(@HeaderParam("X-Amz-Target") String target) {
    72	        if (target != null) {
    73	            return null;
    74	        }
    75	        try {
    76	            List<Bucket> buckets = s3Service.listBuckets();
    77	            XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
    78	                    .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
    79	                    .start("ListAllMyBucketsResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
    80	                    .start("Owner")
    81	                    .elem("ID", "owner")
    82	                    .elem("DisplayName", "owner")
    83	                    .end("Owner")
    84	                    .start("Buckets");
    85	            for (Bucket b : buckets) {
    86	                xml.start("Bucket")
    87	                   .elem("Name", b.getName())
    88	                   .elem("CreationDate", ISO_FORMAT.format(b.getCreationDate()))
    89	                   .end("Bucket");
    90	            }
    91	            xml.end("Buckets").end("ListAllMyBucketsResult");
    92	            return Response.ok(xml.build()).build();
    93	        } catch (AwsException e) {
    94	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
    95	        }
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    @HEAD
    99	    @Path("/{bucket}")
   100	    public Response headBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket) {
   101	        try {
   102	            s3Service.headBucket(bucket);
   103	            String bucketRegion = s3Service.getBucketRegion(bucket);
   104	            if (bucketRegion == null || bucketRegion.isBlank()) {
   105	                bucketRegion = regionResolver.getDefaultRegion();
   106	            }
   107	            return Response.ok()
   108	                    .header("x-amz-bucket-region", bucketRegion)
   109	                    .build();
   110	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   111	            return Response.status(e.getHttpStatus()).build();
   112	        }
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    @PUT
   116	    @Path("/{bucket}")
   117	    public Response createBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   118	                                  @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   119	                                  @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   120	                                  byte[] body) {
   121	        try {
   122	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "notification")) {
   123	                return handlePutBucketNotification(bucket, body);
   124	            }
   125	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "versioning")) {
   126	                return handlePutBucketVersioning(bucket, body);
   127	            }
   128	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   129	                return handlePutBucketTagging(bucket, body);
   130	            }
   131	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "object-lock")) {
   132	                return handlePutObjectLockConfiguration(bucket, body);
   133	            }
   134	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "policy")) {
   135	                s3Service.putBucketPolicy(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   136	                return Response.ok().build();
   137	            }
   138	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "cors")) {
   139	                s3Service.putBucketCors(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   140	                return Response.ok().build();
   141	            }
   142	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "lifecycle")) {
   143	                s3Service.putBucketLifecycle(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   144	                return Response.ok().build();
   145	            }
   146	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "acl")) {
   147	                s3Service.putBucketAcl(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   148	                return Response.ok().build();
   149	            }
   150	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "encryption")) {
   151	                s3Service.putBucketEncryption(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   152	                return Response.ok().build();
   153	            }
   154	
   155	            String locationConstraint = null;
   156	            if (body != null && body.length > 0) {
   157	                locationConstraint = XmlParser.extractFirst(new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8),
   158	                        "LocationConstraint", null);
   159	            }
   160	            if (locationConstraint != null) {
   161	                locationConstraint = locationConstraint.trim();
   162	                if (locationConstraint.isEmpty()) {
   163	                    locationConstraint = null;
   164	                } else if ("us-east-1".equalsIgnoreCase(locationConstraint)) {
   165	                    throw new AwsException("InvalidLocationConstraint",
   166	                            "The specified location-constraint is not valid.", 400);
   167	                }
   168	            }
   169	            String region = locationConstraint != null ? locationConstraint : regionResolver.resolveRegion(httpHeaders);
   170	            s3Service.createBucket(bucket, region);
   171	            String lockEnabled = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-bucket-object-lock-enabled");
   172	            if ("true".equalsIgnoreCase(lockEnabled)) {
   173	                s3Service.putBucketVersioning(bucket, "Enabled");
   174	                s3Service.setBucketObjectLockEnabled(bucket);
   175	            }
   176	            return Response.ok()
   177	                    .header("Location", "/" + bucket)
   178	                    .build();
   179	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   180	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   181	        }

   203	                return Response.noContent().build();

   207	                return Response.noContent().build();

   210	            return Response.noContent().build();

   259	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketAcl(bucket)).build();
   260	            }
   261	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "encryption")) {
   262	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketEncryption(bucket)).build();
   263	            }

   265	            int max = (maxKeys != null && maxKeys > 0) ? maxKeys : 1000;
   266	            List<S3Object> objects = s3Service.listObjects(bucket, prefix, delimiter, max);
   267	            boolean v2 = "2".equals(listType);

   272	                    .elem("Name", bucket)
   273	                    .elem("Prefix", prefix)
   274	                    .elem("Delimiter", delimiter)

   276	            if (v2) {
   277	                xml.elem("KeyCount", objects.size());
   278	            }
   279	            xml.elem("IsTruncated", false);
   280	            for (S3Object obj : objects) {

   284	                   .elem("ETag", obj.getETag())
   285	                   .elem("Size", obj.getSize())
   286	                   .elem("StorageClass", obj.getStorageClass())
   287	                   .end("Contents");

   290	            return Response.ok(xml.build()).build();
   291	        } catch (AwsException e) {

   293	        }
   294	    }

   410	            var resp = Response.ok(obj.getData())
   411	                    .header("Content-Type", obj.getContentType())
   412	                    .header("Content-Length", obj.getSize())
   413	                    .header("ETag", obj.getETag())
   414	                    .header("Last-Modified", RFC_822.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   415	                    .header("Accept-Ranges", "bytes");
   416	            if (obj.getVersionId() != null) {
   417	                resp.header("x-amz-version-id", obj.getVersionId());
   418	            }
   419	            appendObjectHeaders(resp, obj);
   420	            return resp.build();
   421	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   422	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   423	        }
   424	    }
   425	
   426	    private Response handleRangeRequest(S3Object obj, String rangeHeader) {
   427	        byte[] data = obj.getData();
   428	        int totalSize = data.length;
   429	        String rangeSpec = rangeHeader.substring("bytes=".length()).trim();
   430	
   431	        int start, end;
   432	        try {
   433	            int dash = rangeSpec.indexOf('-');
   434	            if (dash < 0) {
   435	                return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   436	            }
   437	            String before = rangeSpec.substring(0, dash);
   438	            String after = rangeSpec.substring(dash + 1);
   439	            if (before.isEmpty() && after.isEmpty()) {
   440	                return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   441	            }
   442	            if (before.isEmpty()) {
   443	                int suffix = Integer.parseInt(after);
   444	                if (suffix <= 0) {
   445	                    return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   446	                }
   447	                start = Math.max(0, totalSize - suffix);
   448	                end = totalSize - 1;
   449	            } else {
   450	                start = Integer.parseInt(before);
   451	                end = after.isEmpty() ? totalSize - 1 : Math.min(Integer.parseInt(after), totalSize - 1);
   452	            }
   453	        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
   454	            return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   455	        }
   456	
   457	        if (start < 0 || start >= totalSize || start > end) {
   458	            return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   459	        }
   460	
   461	        byte[] rangeData = java.util.Arrays.copyOfRange(data, start, end + 1);
   462	        return Response.status(206)
   463	                .entity(rangeData)
   464	                .header("Content-Type", obj.getContentType())
   465	                .header("Content-Length", rangeData.length)
   466	                .header("Content-Range", "bytes " + start + "-" + end + "/" + totalSize)
   467	                .header("ETag", obj.getETag())
   468	                .header("Last-Modified", RFC_822.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   469	                .header("Accept-Ranges", "bytes")
   470	                .build();
   471	    }
   472	
   473	    private Response invalidRangeResponse(int totalSize) {
   474	        String xml = new XmlBuilder()
   475	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   476	                .start("Error")
   477	                .elem("Code", "InvalidRange")
   478	                .elem("Message", "The requested range is not satisfiable.")
   479	                .elem("RequestId", java.util.UUID.randomUUID().toString())
   480	                .end("Error")
   481	                .build();
   482	        return Response.status(416)
   483	                .entity(xml)
   484	                .type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
   485	                .header("Content-Range", "bytes */" + totalSize)
   486	                .build();
   487	    }
   488	
   489	    @HEAD
   490	    @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")
   491	    public Response headObject(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   492	                               @PathParam("key") String key,
   493	                               @QueryParam("versionId") String versionId,
   494	                               @HeaderParam("If-Match") String ifMatch,
   495	                               @HeaderParam("If-None-Match") String ifNoneMatch,
   496	                               @HeaderParam("If-Modified-Since") String ifModifiedSince,
   497	                               @HeaderParam("If-Unmodified-Since") String ifUnmodifiedSince) {
   498	        try {
   499	            S3Object obj = s3Service.headObject(bucket, key, versionId);
   500	            Response preconditionResponse = checkPreconditions(obj, ifMatch, ifNoneMatch, ifModifiedSince, ifUnmodifiedSince);
   501	            if (preconditionResponse != null) {
   502	                return preconditionResponse;
   503	            }
   504	            var resp = Response.ok()
   505	                    .header("Content-Type", obj.getContentType())
   506	                    .header("Content-Length", obj.getSize())
   507	                    .header("ETag", obj.getETag())
   508	                    .header("Last-Modified", RFC_822.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   509	                    .header("Accept-Ranges", "bytes");
   510	            if (obj.getVersionId() != null) {
   511	                resp.header("x-amz-version-id", obj.getVersionId());
   512	            }
   513	            appendObjectHeaders(resp, obj);
   514	            return resp.build();
   515	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   516	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   517	        }
   518	    }

   168	    private S3Object storeObject(String bucketName, String key, byte[] data,
   169	                                 String contentType, Map<String, String> metadata, String storageClass,
   170	                                 S3Checksum checksum, List<Part> parts,
   171	                                 String objectLockMode, Instant retainUntilDate, String legalHoldStatus) {
   172	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   173	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   174	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   175	
   176	        S3Object object = new S3Object(bucketName, key, data, contentType);
   177	        if (metadata != null) {
   178	            object.getMetadata().putAll(metadata);
   179	        }
   180	        object.setStorageClass(ObjectAttributeName.normalizeStorageClass(storageClass));
   181	        object.setChecksum(checksum != null ? copyChecksum(checksum) : buildChecksum(data, parts, false));
   182	        object.setParts(copyParts(parts));
   183	
   184	        if (bucket.isVersioningEnabled()) {
   185	            String versionId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   186	            object.setVersionId(versionId);
   187	            object.setLatest(true);
   188	
   189	            // Check lock protection on the current latest before overwriting
   190	            String latestKey = objectKey(bucketName, key);
   191	            objectStore.get(latestKey).ifPresent(prev -> {
   192	                if (prev.isLatest() && !prev.isDeleteMarker() && bucket.isObjectLockEnabled()) {
   193	                    checkLockProtection(prev, false);
   194	                }
   195	                if (prev.getVersionId() != null) {
   196	                    prev.setLatest(false);
   197	                    objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, prev.getVersionId()), prev);
   198	                }
   199	            });
   200	
   201	            // Apply lock fields from request or bucket default
   202	            applyObjectLock(object, bucket, objectLockMode, retainUntilDate, legalHoldStatus);
   203	
   204	            // Store versioned copy and update latest pointer
   205	            objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId), object);
   206	            objectStore.put(latestKey, object);
   207	            writeFile(bucketName, key, data);
   208	            writeVersionedFile(bucketName, key, versionId, data);
   209	            LOG.debugv("Put versioned object: {0}/{1} v={2} ({3} bytes)", bucketName, key, versionId, data.length);
   210	        } else {
   211	            // Check lock protection on the existing object before overwriting
   212	            if (bucket.isObjectLockEnabled()) {
   213	                objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key)).ifPresent(prev -> {
   214	                    if (!prev.isDeleteMarker()) {
   215	                        checkLockProtection(prev, false);
   216	                    }
   217	                });
   218	            }
   219	
   220	            // Apply lock fields from request or bucket default
   221	            applyObjectLock(object, bucket, objectLockMode, retainUntilDate, legalHoldStatus);
   222	
   223	            objectStore.put(objectKey(bucketName, key), object);
   224	            writeFile(bucketName, key, data);
   225	            LOG.debugv("Put object: {0}/{1} ({2} bytes)", bucketName, key, data.length);
   226	        }
   227	        return object;
   228	    }
   229	
   230	    private void applyObjectLock(S3Object object, Bucket bucket,
   231	                                 String objectLockMode, Instant retainUntilDate, String legalHoldStatus) {
   232	        if (objectLockMode != null) {
   233	            object.setObjectLockMode(objectLockMode);
   234	            object.setRetainUntilDate(retainUntilDate);
   235	        } else if (bucket.isObjectLockEnabled() && bucket.getDefaultRetention() != null) {
   236	            ObjectLockRetention def = bucket.getDefaultRetention();
   237	            object.setObjectLockMode(def.mode());
   238	            long days = "Years".equals(def.unit()) ? (long) def.value() * 365 : def.value();
   239	            object.setRetainUntilDate(Instant.now().plusSeconds(days * 86400L));
   240	        }
   241	        if (legalHoldStatus != null) {
   242	            object.setLegalHoldStatus(legalHoldStatus);
   243	        }
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    private void checkLockProtection(S3Object obj, boolean bypassGovernance) {
   247	        if ("ON".equals(obj.getLegalHoldStatus())) {
   248	            throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object has an active legal hold", 403);
   249	        }
   250	        if (obj.getRetainUntilDate() != null && Instant.now().isBefore(obj.getRetainUntilDate())) {
   251	            if ("COMPLIANCE".equals(obj.getObjectLockMode())) {
   252	                throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object is protected by COMPLIANCE retention", 403);
   253	            }
   254	            if ("GOVERNANCE".equals(obj.getObjectLockMode()) && !bypassGovernance) {
   255	                throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object is protected by GOVERNANCE retention", 403);
   256	            }
   257	        }
   258	    }

   290	    public GetObjectAttributesResult getObjectAttributes(String bucketName, String key, String versionId,
   291	                                                         Set<ObjectAttributeName> attributes,
   292	                                                         Integer maxParts, Integer partNumberMarker) {
   293	        S3Object object = getObjectMetadata(bucketName, key, versionId);
   294	
   295	        GetObjectAttributesResult result = new GetObjectAttributesResult();
   296	        result.setLastModified(object.getLastModified());
   297	        result.setVersionId(object.getVersionId());
   298	
   299	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.E_TAG)) {
   300	            result.setETag(object.getETag());
   301	        }
   302	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.STORAGE_CLASS)) {
   303	            result.setStorageClass(object.getStorageClass());
   304	        }
   305	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.OBJECT_SIZE)) {
   306	            result.setObjectSize(object.getSize());
   307	        }
   308	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.CHECKSUM)) {
   309	            result.setChecksum(copyChecksum(object.getChecksum()));
   310	        }
   311	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.OBJECT_PARTS)) {
   312	            result.setObjectParts(buildObjectParts(object, maxParts, partNumberMarker));
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        return result;
   316	    }

   318	    private S3Object getStoredObject(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
   319	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   320

   326	        if (object.isDeleteMarker()) {
   327	            throw new AwsException("NoSuchKey", "The specified key does not exist.", 404);
   328	        }
   329	        return object;
   330	    }

   361	        return deleteObject(bucketName, key, versionId, false);
   362	    }
   363	
   364	    public S3Object deleteObject(String bucketName, String key, String versionId, boolean bypassGovernance) {
   365	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   366	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   367	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   368	
   369	        if (bucket.isVersioningEnabled() && versionId == null) {
   370	            // Check lock on current latest before placing a delete marker
   371	            objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key)).ifPresent(prev -> {
   372	                if (!prev.isDeleteMarker()) {
   373	                    checkLockProtection(prev, bypassGovernance);
   374	                }
   375	            });
   376	
   377	            // Create a delete marker instead of actually deleting
   378	            S3Object deleteMarker = new S3Object(bucketName, key, new byte[0], null);
   379	            String markerId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   380	            deleteMarker.setVersionId(markerId);
   381	            deleteMarker.setDeleteMarker(true);
   382	            deleteMarker.setLatest(true);
   383	
   384	            // Mark previous latest as not latest
   385	            objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key)).ifPresent(prev -> {
   386	                if (prev.getVersionId() != null) {
   387	                    prev.setLatest(false);
   388	                    objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, prev.getVersionId()), prev);
   389	                }
   390	            });
   391	
   392	            objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, markerId), deleteMarker);
   393	            objectStore.put(objectKey(bucketName, key), deleteMarker);
   394	            LOG.debugv("Created delete marker: {0}/{1} v={2}", bucketName, key, markerId);
   395	            fireNotifications(bucketName, key, "ObjectRemoved:DeleteMarkerCreated", deleteMarker);
   396	            return deleteMarker;
   397	        } else if (versionId != null) {
   398	            // Check lock on the specific version before permanent deletion
   399	            objectStore.get(versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId)).ifPresent(obj -> {
   400	                if (!obj.isDeleteMarker()) {
   401	                    checkLockProtection(obj, bypassGovernance);
   402	                }
   403	            });
   404	            // Permanently delete a specific version
   405	            objectStore.delete(versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId));
   406	            LOG.debugv("Permanently deleted version: {0}/{1} v={2}", bucketName, key, versionId);
   407	            return null;
   408	        } else {
   409	            // Check lock on the non-versioned object before delete
   410	            objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key)).ifPresent(obj -> {
   411	                if (!obj.isDeleteMarker()) {
   412	                    checkLockProtection(obj, bypassGovernance);
   413	                }
   414	            });
   415	            // Non-versioned delete
   416	            objectStore.delete(objectKey(bucketName, key));
   417	            deleteFile(bucketName, key);
   418	            LOG.debugv("Deleted object: {0}/{1}", bucketName, key);
   419	            fireNotifications(bucketName, key, "ObjectRemoved:Delete", null);
   420	            return null;
   421	        }
   422	    }
   423	
   424	    public List<S3Object> listObjects(String bucketName, String prefix, String delimiter, int maxKeys) {
   425	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   426	
   427	        String keyPrefix = bucketName + "/";
   428	        String fullPrefix = prefix != null ? keyPrefix + prefix : keyPrefix;
   429	
   430	        // Filter out versioned entries (contain #v#) and delete markers
   431	        List<S3Object> allObjects = objectStore.scan(key ->
   432	                        key.startsWith(fullPrefix) && !key.contains("#v#"))
   433	                .stream()
   434	                .filter(obj -> !obj.isDeleteMarker())
   435	                .toList();
   436	        allObjects = new ArrayList<>(allObjects);
   437	
   438	        if (delimiter != null && !delimiter.isEmpty()) {
   439	            // Filter to only return objects at this level (simulate directory listing)
   440	            allObjects = allObjects.stream()
   441	                    .filter(obj -> {
   442	                        String remainder = obj.getKey().substring(prefix != null ? prefix.length() : 0);
   443	                        return !remainder.contains(delimiter);
   444	                    })
   445	                    .toList();
   446	        }
   447	
   448	        if (maxKeys > 0 && allObjects.size() > maxKeys) {
   449	            allObjects = allObjects.subList(0, maxKeys);
   450	        }

   455	    public S3Object copyObject(String sourceBucket, String sourceKey,
   456	                               String destBucket, String destKey) {
   457	        return copyObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey, destBucket, destKey,
   458	                null, null, null, null);
   459	    }
   460	
   461	    public S3Object copyObject(String sourceBucket, String sourceKey,
   462	                               String destBucket, String destKey,
   463	                               String metadataDirective, Map<String, String> replacementMetadata,
   464	                               String storageClass, String contentType) {
   465	        S3Object source = getObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey);
   466	        ensureBucketExists(destBucket);
   467	
   468	        boolean replaceMetadata = "REPLACE".equalsIgnoreCase(metadataDirective);
   469	        Map<String, String> metadata = replaceMetadata ? new LinkedHashMap<>() : new LinkedHashMap<>(source.getMetadata());
   470	        if (replaceMetadata && replacementMetadata != null) {
   471	            metadata.putAll(replacementMetadata);
   472	        }
   473	
   474	        String effectiveContentType = replaceMetadata && contentType != null ? contentType : source.getContentType();
   475	        String effectiveStorageClass = storageClass != null ? storageClass : source.getStorageClass();
   476	        S3Object copy = storeObject(destBucket, destKey, source.getData(), effectiveContentType, metadata,
   477	                effectiveStorageClass, source.getChecksum(), source.getParts(), null, null, null);
   478	        copy.setETag(source.getETag());
   479	        LOG.debugv("Copied object: {0}/{1} -> {2}/{3}", sourceBucket, sourceKey, destBucket, destKey);
   480	        fireNotifications(destBucket, destKey, "ObjectCreated:Copy", copy);
   481	        return copy;
   482	    }

   484	    // --- Versioning Operations ---
   485	
   486	    public void putBucketVersioning(String bucketName, String status) {
   487	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   488	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   489	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   490	        if (!"Enabled".equals(status) && !"Suspended".equals(status)) {
   491	            throw new AwsException("MalformedXML",
   492	                    "Versioning status must be 'Enabled' or 'Suspended'.", 400);
   493	        }
   494	        bucket.setVersioningStatus(status);
   495	        bucketStore.put(bucketName, bucket);
   496	        LOG.infov("Set versioning for bucket {0}: {1}", bucketName, status);
   497	    }
   498	
   499	    public String getBucketVersioning(String bucketName) {
   500	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   501	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   502	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   503	        return bucket.getVersioningStatus();
   504	    }
   505	
   506	    public List<S3Object> listObjectVersions(String bucketName, String prefix, int maxKeys) {
   507	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   508	
   509	        String versionPrefix = bucketName + "/";
   510	        String fullPrefix = prefix != null ? versionPrefix + prefix : versionPrefix;
   511	
   512	        // Scan for versioned entries (contain #v#)
   513	        List<S3Object> versions = new ArrayList<>(objectStore.scan(key ->
   514	                key.startsWith(fullPrefix) && key.contains("#v#")));
   515	
   516	        // Sort by key, then by lastModified descending
   517	        versions.sort((a, b) -> {
   518	            int keyCompare = a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
   519	            if (keyCompare != 0) return keyCompare;
   520	            return b.getLastModified().compareTo(a.getLastModified());
   521	        });
   522	
   523	        if (maxKeys > 0 && versions.size() > maxKeys) {
   524	            versions = versions.subList(0, maxKeys);
   525	        }
   526	        return versions;
   527	    }

  1049	    private Response handleCopyObject(String copySource, String destBucket, String destKey,
  1050	                                      String contentType, HttpHeaders httpHeaders) {
  1051	        String source = copySource.startsWith("/") ? copySource.substring(1) : copySource;
  1052	        int slashIndex = source.indexOf('/');
  1053	        if (slashIndex < 0) {
  1054	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgument", "Invalid copy source: " + copySource, 400);
  1055	        }
  1056	        String sourceBucket = source.substring(0, slashIndex);
  1057	        String sourceKey = URLDecoder.decode(source.substring(slashIndex + 1), StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
  1058

  1060	                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-metadata-directive"),
  1061	                extractUserMetadata(httpHeaders),
  1062	                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-storage-class"),
  1063	                contentType);
  1064	        String xml = new XmlBuilder()
  1065	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
  1066	                .start("CopyObjectResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
  1067	                .elem("LastModified", ISO_FORMAT.format(copy.getLastModified()))
  1068	                .elem("ETag", copy.getETag())
  1069	                .end("CopyObjectResult")
  1070	                .build();
  1071	        return Response.ok(xml).build();
  1072	    }
  1073	
  1074	    private Response handleGetObjectAttributes(String bucket, String key, String versionId,
  1075	                                               String objectAttributesHeader, Integer maxParts,
  1076	                                               Integer partNumberMarker) {
  1077	        Set<ObjectAttributeName> attributes = ObjectAttributeName.parseHeader(objectAttributesHeader);
  1078	        GetObjectAttributesResult result = s3Service.getObjectAttributes(bucket, key, versionId,
  1079	                attributes, maxParts, partNumberMarker);
  1080	
  1081	        XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
  1082	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
  1083	                .start("GetObjectAttributesResponse", AwsNamespaces.S3)
  1084	                .elem("ETag", result.getETag());
  1085	        appendChecksum(xml, result.getChecksum());
  1086	        appendObjectParts(xml, result.getObjectParts());
  1087	        if (result.getStorageClass() != null) {
  1088	            xml.elem("StorageClass", result.getStorageClass());
  1089	        }
  1090	        if (result.getObjectSize() != null) {
  1091	            xml.elem("ObjectSize", result.getObjectSize());
  1092	        }
  1093	        xml.end("GetObjectAttributesResponse");
  1094	
  1095	        Response.ResponseBuilder response = Response.ok(xml.build()).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML);
  1096	        if (result.getLastModified() != null) {
  1097	            response.header("Last-Modified", RFC_822.format(result.getLastModified()));
  1098	        }
  1099	        if (result.getVersionId() != null) {
  1100	            response.header("x-amz-version-id", result.getVersionId());
  1101	        }
  1102	        return response.build();
  1103	    }
  1104	
  1105	    private void appendChecksum(XmlBuilder xml, S3Checksum checksum) {
  1106	        if (checksum == null || !checksum.hasAnyValue()) {
  1107	            return;
  1108	        }
  1109	        xml.start("Checksum")
  1110	                .elem("ChecksumCRC32", checksum.getChecksumCRC32())
  1111	                .elem("ChecksumCRC32C", checksum.getChecksumCRC32C())
  1112	                .elem("ChecksumCRC64NVME", checksum.getChecksumCRC64NVME())
  1113	                .elem("ChecksumSHA1", checksum.getChecksumSHA1())
  1114	                .elem("ChecksumSHA256", checksum.getChecksumSHA256())
  1115	                .elem("ChecksumType", checksum.getChecksumType())
  1116	                .end("Checksum");
  1117	    }
  1118

  1120	        if (objectParts == null) {

   170	                                 S3Checksum checksum, List<Part> parts,
   171	                                 String objectLockMode, Instant retainUntilDate, String legalHoldStatus) {
   172	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   173	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   174	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   175	
   176	        S3Object object = new S3Object(bucketName, key, data, contentType);
   177	        if (metadata != null) {
   178	            object.getMetadata().putAll(metadata);
   179	        }
   180	        object.setStorageClass(ObjectAttributeName.normalizeStorageClass(storageClass));
   181	        object.setChecksum(checksum != null ? copyChecksum(checksum) : buildChecksum(data, parts, false));
   182	        object.setParts(copyParts(parts));
   183	
   184	        if (bucket.isVersioningEnabled()) {
   185	            String versionId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   186	            object.setVersionId(versionId);
   187	            object.setLatest(true);
   188	
   189	            // Check lock protection on the current latest before overwriting
   190	            String latestKey = objectKey(bucketName, key);
   191	            objectStore.get(latestKey).ifPresent(prev -> {
   192	                if (prev.isLatest() && !prev.isDeleteMarker() && bucket.isObjectLockEnabled()) {
   193	                    checkLockProtection(prev, false);
   194	                }
   195	                if (prev.getVersionId() != null) {
   196	                    prev.setLatest(false);
   197	                    objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, prev.getVersionId()), prev);
   198	                }
   199	            });
   200	
   201	            // Apply lock fields from request or bucket default
   202	            applyObjectLock(object, bucket, objectLockMode, retainUntilDate, legalHoldStatus);
   203	
   204	            // Store versioned copy and update latest pointer
   205	            objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId), object);
   206	            objectStore.put(latestKey, object);
   207	            writeFile(bucketName, key, data);
   208	            writeVersionedFile(bucketName, key, versionId, data);
   209	            LOG.debugv("Put versioned object: {0}/{1} v={2} ({3} bytes)", bucketName, key, versionId, data.length);
   210	        } else {
   211	            // Check lock protection on the existing object before overwriting
   212	            if (bucket.isObjectLockEnabled()) {
   213	                objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key)).ifPresent(prev -> {
   214	                    if (!prev.isDeleteMarker()) {
   215	                        checkLockProtection(prev, false);
   216	                    }
   217	                });
   218	            }
   219	
   220	            // Apply lock fields from request or bucket default
   221	            applyObjectLock(object, bucket, objectLockMode, retainUntilDate, legalHoldStatus);
   222	
   223	            objectStore.put(objectKey(bucketName, key), object);
   224	            writeFile(bucketName, key, data);
   225	            LOG.debugv("Put object: {0}/{1} ({2} bytes)", bucketName, key, data.length);
   226	        }
   227	        return object;
   228	    }
   229	
   230	    private void applyObjectLock(S3Object object, Bucket bucket,

    public MultipartUpload initiateMultipartUpload(String bucket, String key, String contentType,
                                                   Map<String, String> metadata, String storageClass) {
        ensureBucketExists(bucket);
        MultipartUpload upload = new MultipartUpload(bucket, key, contentType);
        if (metadata != null) {
            upload.getMetadata().putAll(metadata);
        }
        upload.setStorageClass(ObjectAttributeName.normalizeStorageClass(storageClass));

            memoryMultipartStore.put(upload.getUploadId(), new ConcurrentHashMap<>());

            } catch (IOException e) {

   235	
   236	        S3Object stored = s3Service.putObject("test-bucket", "docs/file.txt", "payload".getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8),

   238	
   239	        S3Object head = s3Service.headObject("test-bucket", "docs/file.txt");
   240	        assertEquals("STANDARD_IA", head.getStorageClass());
   241	        assertEquals("team-a", head.getMetadata().get("owner"));
   242	        assertNotNull(head.getChecksum());
   243	        assertNotNull(head.getChecksum().getChecksumSHA256());
   244	        assertEquals("FULL_OBJECT", head.getChecksum().getChecksumType());
   245	        assertEquals(stored.getETag(), head.getETag());

   252	                "text/plain", Map.of("env", "dev"), "GLACIER", null, null, null);
   253	
   254	        GetObjectAttributesResult attributes = s3Service.getObjectAttributes("test-bucket", "report.txt", null,
   255	                Set.of(ObjectAttributeName.E_TAG, ObjectAttributeName.OBJECT_SIZE,
   256	                        ObjectAttributeName.STORAGE_CLASS, ObjectAttributeName.CHECKSUM),
   257	                null, null);

   260	        assertEquals(7L, attributes.getObjectSize());
   261	        assertEquals("GLACIER", attributes.getStorageClass());
   262	        assertNotNull(attributes.getChecksum());
   263	        assertNotNull(attributes.getChecksum().getChecksumSHA256());
   264	        assertNull(attributes.getObjectParts());

All the changes look correct. Let me summarize what was changed:

1. **`S3Object.java`**: Added `contentEncoding` field with getter and setter
2. **`MultipartUpload.java`**: Added `contentEncoding` field with getter and setter 
3. **`S3Service.java`**: 
   - Added a new overload of `putObject` that accepts `contentEncoding` (with backward-compatible old signatures preserved)
   - Updated `storeObject` to accept and store `contentEncoding`
   - Updated `copyObject` to preserve `contentEncoding` from source (unless replaced)
   - Updated `initiateMultipartUpload` to accept and store `contentEncoding`
   - Updated `completeMultipartUpload` to pass `contentEncoding` from the multipart upload to the final object
   - Updated private `copyObject` helper to copy `contentEncoding`
4. **`S3Controller.java`**:
   - Updated `putObject` to pass the `contentEncoding` header to `s3Service.putObject`
   - Updated multipart upload initiation to pass `Content-Encoding` header
   - Updated `appendObjectHeaders` to include `Content-Encoding` header in responses

Now let me think about edge cases:

1. **Null contentEncoding**: Handled - if not provided, it's null and the header won't be included in responses (the `appendObjectHeaders` checks for null).
2. **Copy with metadata replace**: When `REPLACE` directive is used, content-encoding is set to null (intentional - it's a metadata replacement).
3. **Multipart upload**: Content-encoding is preserved from the initial upload through to the final object.
4. **Versioning**: Content-encoding is stored on the versioned object correctly since it goes through `storeObject`.
5. **Presigned POST upload**: Uses the old `putObject` signature that defaults contentEncoding to null - this is correct.
